import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { 
  FileText, Sparkles, RefreshCw, HelpCircle, Plus, Trash2, Link, 
  CheckCircle2, AlertCircle, BookOpen, Edit3, ArrowRightLeft, Camera, Layers,
  Maximize2, Minimize2
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Slide } from '../types';

interface ScreenplayWriterProps {
  slides: Slide[];
  onUpdateSlides: (newSlides: Slide[]) => void;
  folderName: string;
  activeSlideId: string | null;
  onSelectSlideId: (id: string | null) => void;
  isFullScreen?: boolean;
  onToggleFullScreen?: () => void;
}

export interface ScriptParagraph {
  type: 'scene-heading' | 'action' | 'character' | 'dialogue' | 'parenthetical' | 'transition' | 'frame-tag' | 'empty';
  text: string;
  sceneNo?: number;
  shotNo?: number;
}

// Client-side parser for Screenplay (Fountain-light format)
export function parseScreenplay(text: string): ScriptParagraph[] {
  const lines = text.split('\n');
  const paragraphs: ScriptParagraph[] = [];
  
  for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    const line = lines[i].trim();
    if (!line) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'empty', text: '' });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for frame tags: [Frame: Scene X, Shot Y] or [Frame: Sc X, Sh Y]
    const frameMatch = line.match(/\[Frame:\s*(?:Scene|Sc)?\s*(\d+)\s*,\s*(?:Shot|Sh)?\s*(\d+)\]/i);
    if (frameMatch) {
      paragraphs.push({
        type: 'frame-tag',
        text: line,
        sceneNo: parseInt(frameMatch[1], 10),
        shotNo: parseInt(frameMatch[2], 10)
      });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for scene heading
    if (line.match(/^(?:INT|EXT|INT\/EXT|EXT\/INT|I\/E)\.?\s+/i)) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'scene-heading', text: line.toUpperCase() });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for transitions
    if (line.match(/^(?:FADE IN|FADE OUT|CUT TO|DISSOLVE TO|FADE TO BLACK|FADE TO)\s*:/i) || line.toUpperCase().endsWith('TO:')) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'transition', text: line.toUpperCase() });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Check for Character / Dialogue sequence
    const isAllCaps = line === line.toUpperCase() && /[A-Z]/.test(line);
    if (isAllCaps) {
      // Look ahead to see if there is dialogue
      let nextLine = '';
      for (let j = i + 1; j < lines.length; j++) {
        const testLine = lines[j].trim();
        if (testLine) {
          nextLine = testLine;
          break;
        }
      }
      
      if (nextLine) {
        paragraphs.push({ type: 'character', text: line });
        continue;
      }
    }
    
    // Check for parenthetical
    if (line.startsWith('(') && line.endsWith(')')) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'parenthetical', text: line });
      continue;
    }
    
    // Default is dialogue if previous was character or parenthetical
    const prevParagraph = paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 1];
    if (prevParagraph && (prevParagraph.type === 'character' || prevParagraph.type === 'parenthetical' || (prevParagraph.type === 'empty' && paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 2] && (paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 2].type === 'character' || paragraphs[paragraphs.length - 2].type === 'parenthetical')))) {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'dialogue', text: line });
    } else {
      paragraphs.push({ type: 'action', text: line });
    }
  }
  
  return paragraphs;
}

export default function ScreenplayWriter({
  slides,
  onUpdateSlides,
  folderName,
  activeSlideId,
  onSelectSlideId,
  isFullScreen = false,
  onToggleFullScreen
}: ScreenplayWriterProps) {
  const [scriptText, setScriptText] = useState<string>(() => {
    return localStorage.getItem('storyboard_screenplay_text') || '';
  });
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'edit' | 'preview'>('edit');
  const [isGenerating, setIsGenerating] = useState(false);
  const [isExtracting, setIsExtracting] = useState(false);
  const [errorMsg, setErrorMsg] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [infoMsg, setInfoMsg] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showHelp, setShowHelp] = useState(false);
  const [highlightedFrameKey, setHighlightedFrameKey] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [isAIEnabled, setIsAIEnabled] = useState(false);
  const textareaRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);

  // Save changes to local storage
  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('storyboard_screenplay_text', scriptText);
  }, [scriptText]);

  // Sync highlighting from selected Storyboard frame
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeSlideId) {
      const slide = slides.find(s => s.id === activeSlideId);
      if (slide) {
        const key = `${slide.sceneNo}-${slide.shotNo}`;
        setHighlightedFrameKey(key);
        // Automatically set info message
        setInfoMsg(`Correlated to Scene ${slide.sceneNo}, Shot ${slide.shotNo}`);
        setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 3000);
      }
    } else {
      setHighlightedFrameKey(null);
    }
  }, [activeSlideId, slides]);

  // AI: Generate Screenplay based on current slides
  const handleAIGenerateScript = async () => {
    if (slides.length === 0) {
      setErrorMsg('Add at least one storyboard slide to generate a screenplay.');
      return;
    }
    
    setIsGenerating(true);
    setErrorMsg(null);
    setInfoMsg(null);

    try {
      const simplifiedSlides = slides.map(s => ({
        sceneNo: s.sceneNo,
        shotNo: s.shotNo,
        shotType: s.shotType || 'MS',
        action: s.action || '',
        dialogue: s.dialogue || '',
        notes: s.notes || '',
        duration: s.duration || 3000
      }));

      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/generate-script', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ slides: simplifiedSlides, folderName })
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to generate script');
      }

      if (data.script) {
        setScriptText(data.script);
        setInfoMsg('AI Screenplay Generated successfully!');
        setActiveTab('preview');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error(err);
      setErrorMsg(err.message || 'AI generation failed. Check your API key configuration.');
    } finally {
      setIsGenerating(false);
    }
  };

  // AI: Extract slides from current script text
  const handleAIExtractFrames = async () => {
    if (!scriptText.trim()) {
      setErrorMsg('Please write or generate a screenplay script first.');
      return;
    }

    setIsExtracting(true);
    setErrorMsg(null);
    setInfoMsg(null);

    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/extract-frames', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ scriptText })
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to extract frames');
      }

      if (data.frames && Array.isArray(data.frames)) {
        // Map the extracted JSON blocks to slides
        const newSlides: Slide[] = data.frames.map((f: any, idx: number) => ({
          id: `extracted-${Date.now()}-${idx}`,
          sceneNo: Number(f.sceneNo) || 1,
          shotNo: Number(f.shotNo) || (idx + 1),
          shotType: f.shotType || 'MS',
          duration: Number(f.duration) || 3000,
          action: f.action || '',
          dialogue: f.dialogue || '',
          notes: f.notes || '',
          imageUrl: 'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1536440136628-849c177e76a1?w=800&auto=format&fit=crop&q=60', // placeholder cinematic image
          imageScale: 1,
          fitMode: 'cover'
        }));

        if (confirm(`AI extracted ${newSlides.length} visual shots from the screenplay. Do you want to append them to your Storyboard deck?`)) {
          const merged = [...slides, ...newSlides];
          onUpdateSlides(merged);
          setInfoMsg(`Successfully appended ${newSlides.length} cinematic frames!`);
        }
      } else {
        throw new Error('AI response was invalid or contained no frames.');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      console.error(err);
      setErrorMsg(err.message || 'AI extraction failed. Check your API key.');
    } finally {
      setIsExtracting(false);
    }
  };

  // Link slide to current cursor position inside script
  const handleInsertFrameTag = (slide: Slide) => {
    if (!textareaRef.current) return;
    
    const textarea = textareaRef.current;
    const start = textarea.selectionStart;
    const end = textarea.selectionEnd;
    const text = textarea.value;
    
    const tag = `\n[Frame: Scene ${slide.sceneNo}, Shot ${slide.shotNo}]\n`;
    const newText = text.substring(0, start) + tag + text.substring(end);
    
    setScriptText(newText);
    
    // Reset cursor
    setTimeout(() => {
      textarea.focus();
      textarea.setSelectionRange(start + tag.length, start + tag.length);
    }, 100);
    
    setInfoMsg(`Inserted tag [Scene ${slide.sceneNo}, Shot ${slide.shotNo}]`);
    setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 3000);
  };

  // Sync narrative action/dialogues from Screenplay back to Storyboard slides!
  const handleSyncToStoryboard = () => {
    const paragraphs = parseScreenplay(scriptText);
    let updatedCount = 0;
    const newSlides = [...slides];

    for (let i = 0; i < paragraphs.length; i++) {
      const p = paragraphs[i];
      if (p.type === 'frame-tag' && p.sceneNo !== undefined && p.shotNo !== undefined) {
        // Find matching slide in storyboard
        const slideIndex = newSlides.findIndex(s => s.sceneNo === p.sceneNo && s.shotNo === p.shotNo);
        if (slideIndex !== -1) {
          // Gather succeeding action & dialogue paragraphs until the next frame tag or scene heading
          let accumulatedAction = '';
          let accumulatedDialogue = '';
          
          for (let j = i + 1; j < paragraphs.length; j++) {
            const nextP = paragraphs[j];
            if (nextP.type === 'frame-tag' || nextP.type === 'scene-heading') {
              break;
            }
            if (nextP.type === 'action' && nextP.text) {
              accumulatedAction += (accumulatedAction ? ' ' : '') + nextP.text;
            }
            if (nextP.type === 'dialogue' && nextP.text) {
              accumulatedDialogue += (accumulatedDialogue ? ' ' : '') + nextP.text;
            }
          }

          // Update slide if we found matching text
          let changed = false;
          if (accumulatedAction && newSlides[slideIndex].action !== accumulatedAction) {
            newSlides[slideIndex].action = accumulatedAction;
            changed = true;
          }
          if (accumulatedDialogue && newSlides[slideIndex].dialogue !== accumulatedDialogue) {
            newSlides[slideIndex].dialogue = accumulatedDialogue;
            changed = true;
          }
          
          if (changed) {
            updatedCount++;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (updatedCount > 0) {
      onUpdateSlides(newSlides);
      setInfoMsg(`Synced & updated visual cues in ${updatedCount} matching storyboard frames!`);
    } else {
      setInfoMsg('No updates found. Verify you have matching [Frame: Scene X, Shot Y] tags in your script.');
    }
    setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 5000);
  };

  // Interactive frame link click
  const handleFrameTagClick = (sceneNo: number, shotNo: number) => {
    const match = slides.find(s => s.sceneNo === sceneNo && s.shotNo === shotNo);
    if (match) {
      onSelectSlideId(match.id);
      setHighlightedFrameKey(`${sceneNo}-${shotNo}`);
      setInfoMsg(`Jumping to Storyboard Scene ${sceneNo}, Shot ${shotNo}`);
      setTimeout(() => setInfoMsg(null), 3000);
    } else {
      setErrorMsg(`No storyboard slide matches Scene ${sceneNo}, Shot ${shotNo}`);
      setTimeout(() => setErrorMsg(null), 4000);
    }
  };

  const parsedParagraphs = parseScreenplay(scriptText);

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full bg-[#0E0E12] bg-theme-panel border-l border-neutral-800 border-theme text-xs">
      {/* Sidebar Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-neutral-850 border-theme bg-neutral-900/40 bg-theme-badge shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" />
          <h3 className="font-black text-white text-sm">Screenplay Suite</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
          {onToggleFullScreen && (
            <button
              onClick={onToggleFullScreen}
              className="p-1 text-neutral-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-neutral-800 rounded transition-colors mr-1 cursor-pointer"
              title={isFullScreen ? "Exit Fullscreen" : "Fullscreen Screenplay Mode"}
            >
              {isFullScreen ? <Minimize2 className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" /> : <Maximize2 className="w-4 h-4" />}
            </button>
          )}
          <button 
            onClick={() => setShowHelp(!showHelp)}
            className="p-1 text-neutral-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-neutral-800 rounded transition-colors cursor-pointer"
            title="Screenplay formatting help"
          >
            <HelpCircle className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Screenplay Formatting Guide banner */}
      {showHelp && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-indigo-950/20 border-b border-indigo-500/20 text-neutral-300 animate-fade-in shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1.5">
            <span className="font-bold text-indigo-300 uppercase text-[9px] tracking-wider">Typewriter Guide</span>
            <button onClick={() => setShowHelp(false)} className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 hover:text-white font-black">Close</button>
          </div>
          <ul className="space-y-1 text-[11px] list-disc list-inside text-neutral-400">
            <li><strong className="text-white font-mono text-[10px]">INT. / EXT. COFFEE SHOP</strong> starts a Scene heading.</li>
            <li><strong className="text-white font-mono text-[10px]">CHARACTER (ALL CAPS)</strong> on its own line signals character.</li>
            <li>Indented dialogues and italicized parentheticals auto-format.</li>
            <li>Use <strong className="text-indigo-400 font-mono text-[10px]">[Frame: Scene 1, Shot 2]</strong> to link a visual slide.</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Alert Messaging area */}
      {errorMsg && (
        <div className="p-2 bg-rose-950/20 border-b border-rose-500/20 text-rose-400 text-[11px] flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0 animate-fade-in">
          <AlertCircle className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0" />
          <span className="truncate flex-1">{errorMsg}</span>
          <button onClick={() => setErrorMsg(null)} className="font-black text-[9px] px-1 hover:text-white">✕</button>
        </div>
      )}

      {infoMsg && (
        <div className="p-2 bg-emerald-950/20 border-b border-emerald-500/20 text-emerald-400 text-[11px] flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0 animate-fade-in">
          <CheckCircle2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 text-emerald-400" />
          <span className="truncate flex-1">{infoMsg}</span>
          <button onClick={() => setInfoMsg(null)} className="font-black text-[9px] px-1 hover:text-white">✕</button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Toolbar Options */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 bg-neutral-900/60 border-b border-neutral-850 shrink-0">
        {/* Toggle Mode */}
        <div className="flex bg-neutral-950 p-0.5 rounded-lg border border-neutral-850">
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('edit')}
            className={`px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md text-[10px] font-black uppercase transition-all flex items-center gap-1 ${
              activeTab === 'edit' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow-md' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Edit3 className="w-3 h-3" /> Typewriter
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('preview')}
            className={`px-2.5 py-1 rounded-md text-[10px] font-black uppercase transition-all flex items-center gap-1 ${
              activeTab === 'preview' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow-md' : 'text-neutral-400 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <BookOpen className="w-3 h-3" /> Cinematic Preview
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Action button bar */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <button
            onClick={handleSyncToStoryboard}
            disabled={slides.length === 0 || !scriptText}
            className="flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 bg-indigo-950/40 hover:bg-indigo-950/60 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/20 hover:border-indigo-500/40 rounded text-[10px] font-bold transition-all disabled:opacity-40 cursor-pointer shrink-0"
            title="Parse screenplay changes and push action/dialogue back to matching storyboard frames"
          >
            <ArrowRightLeft className="w-3 h-3 text-indigo-400" /> Sync to Board
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Primary Workstation Pane */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden relative flex flex-col">
        {activeTab === 'edit' ? (
          <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
            <textarea
              ref={textareaRef}
              value={scriptText}
              onChange={(e) => setScriptText(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={`Write your cinematic screenplay here...\n\nExample:\n\nFADE IN:\n\nINT. COFFEE SHOP - DAY\n\n[Frame: Scene 1, Shot 1]\nHERO sits nervously holding a warm mug. The steam rises gently.\n\nHERO\nIs there anyone else coming?`}
              className="flex-1 w-full bg-[#09090D] bg-theme-app text-neutral-200 text-theme-primary p-4 font-mono text-xs leading-relaxed outline-none border-none resize-none overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar"
              style={{ tabSize: 4 }}
            />
          </div>
        ) : (
          /* CINEMATIC PREVIEW TAB (Fountain styled screenplay) */
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 bg-[#09090D] bg-theme-app text-neutral-300 text-theme-primary font-mono leading-loose custom-scrollbar selection:bg-indigo-600/30">
            {parsedParagraphs.length === 0 || (parsedParagraphs.length === 1 && parsedParagraphs[0].type === 'empty') ? (
              <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center p-4 text-neutral-500 text-theme-muted">
                <FileText className="w-8 h-8 text-neutral-600 mb-2" />
                <p className="text-xs">Your screenplay screenplay is empty.</p>
                <p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 mt-1">Switch to typewriter mode to draft your cinematic project.</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="max-w-md mx-auto space-y-1 pb-16 text-[11.5px]">
                {parsedParagraphs.map((p, idx) => {
                  const isHighlighted = p.sceneNo !== undefined && p.shotNo !== undefined && highlightedFrameKey === `${p.sceneNo}-${p.shotNo}`;
                  
                  if (p.type === 'empty') {
                    return <div key={idx} className="h-4" />;
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'frame-tag') {
                    return (
                      <div 
                        key={idx} 
                        onClick={() => handleFrameTagClick(p.sceneNo!, p.shotNo!)}
                        className={`my-3 p-2 rounded-lg border flex items-center justify-between cursor-pointer transition-all ${
                          isHighlighted 
                            ? 'bg-indigo-600/15 border-indigo-500/55 text-indigo-400 shadow-md ring-1 ring-indigo-500/20' 
                            : 'bg-neutral-900/60 bg-theme-panel border-neutral-800 border-theme text-neutral-300 hover:border-indigo-500/50 hover:bg-neutral-900 text-theme-primary'
                        }`}
                      >
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 font-sans font-extrabold text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider">
                          <Camera className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${isHighlighted ? 'text-indigo-400' : 'text-neutral-500 text-theme-muted'}`} />
                          <span>Frame Visual: Scene {p.sceneNo}, Shot {p.shotNo}</span>
                        </div>
                        <span className="font-sans font-black text-[9px] uppercase tracking-widest px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-neutral-800/80 rounded hover:bg-indigo-600 hover:text-white transition-colors">Select Frame</span>
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'scene-heading') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-white pt-4 pb-1 border-b border-neutral-800 border-theme mb-2">
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'character') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-center font-bold text-indigo-400 uppercase pt-2" style={{ width: '80%', margin: '0 auto' }}>
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'parenthetical') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-center italic text-neutral-400 text-theme-muted" style={{ width: '60%', margin: '0 auto' }}>
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'dialogue') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-neutral-200 text-theme-primary" style={{ width: '70%', margin: '0 auto', textAlign: 'left', textIndent: '0' }}>
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  if (p.type === 'transition') {
                    return (
                      <div key={idx} className="text-right font-bold uppercase py-2 text-neutral-400 text-theme-muted">
                        {p.text}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }

                  // Default Action
                  return (
                    <div key={idx} className="text-neutral-300 text-theme-primary leading-relaxed text-justify">
                      {p.text}
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Frame Insertion Panel (bottom) */}
      <div className="p-3 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-900/50 shrink-0">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
          <span className="text-[10px] font-black text-neutral-400 uppercase tracking-widest">Story Deck Link</span>
          <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-neutral-600">{slides.length} Frames Available</span>
        </div>
        
        {slides.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="p-3 border border-dashed border-neutral-800 rounded-lg text-center text-neutral-500 text-[11px]">
            No storyboard slides available.
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1.5 custom-scrollbar">
            {slides.map((s, index) => {
              const isSelected = s.id === activeSlideId;
              return (
                <button
                  key={s.id}
                  onClick={() => {
                    onSelectSlideId(s.id);
                    handleInsertFrameTag(s);
                  }}
                  className={`flex-none w-16 group relative border rounded-lg overflow-hidden bg-black transition-all cursor-pointer ${
                    isSelected ? 'border-indigo-500 scale-[1.02]' : 'border-neutral-800 hover:border-neutral-600'
                  }`}
                  title={`Insert [Frame: Scene ${s.sceneNo}, Shot ${s.shotNo}] tag at cursor`}
                >
                  <div className="aspect-video w-full overflow-hidden relative bg-neutral-900">
                    <img src={s.imageUrl} alt="" className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
                    <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/40 group-hover:bg-black/15 transition-all" />
                    <div className="absolute bottom-1 left-1 px-1 bg-black/70 rounded text-[8px] font-mono font-black text-white">
                      S{s.sceneNo}.H{s.shotNo}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="py-0.5 text-center text-[8px] font-extrabold uppercase bg-neutral-950 text-neutral-400 group-hover:text-white truncate">
                    + Insert
                  </div>
                </button>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Enhanced Screenplay Writer (AI Writer) toggle */}
      <div className="px-3 py-2 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-950/90 shrink-0 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <Sparkles className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 ${isAIEnabled ? "text-indigo-400 animate-pulse" : "text-neutral-500"}`} />
          <div className="flex flex-col">
            <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-neutral-300 uppercase tracking-wider">Enhanced AI Screenplay</span>
            <span className="text-[8px] font-medium text-neutral-500">Enable automated AI drafting & shot extraction</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setIsAIEnabled(!isAIEnabled)}
          className={`relative inline-flex h-4 w-8 shrink-0 cursor-pointer rounded-full border-2 border-transparent transition-colors duration-200 ease-in-out outline-none ${
            isAIEnabled ? "bg-indigo-600" : "bg-neutral-800"
          }`}
          title={isAIEnabled ? "Disable AI Assistant" : "Enable AI Assistant"}
        >
          <span
            className={`pointer-events-none inline-block h-3 w-3 transform rounded-full bg-white shadow ring-0 transition duration-200 ease-in-out ${
              isAIEnabled ? "translate-x-4" : "translate-x-0"
            }`}
          />
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* AI Assistant footer actions */}
      <div className="p-3 border-t border-neutral-850 bg-neutral-950 shrink-0 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
        <button
          onClick={handleAIGenerateScript}
          disabled={!isAIEnabled || isGenerating || slides.length === 0}
          className={`flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider transition-all cursor-pointer shadow-md ${
            isAIEnabled 
              ? "bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white" 
              : "bg-neutral-900 text-neutral-500 border border-neutral-850/60 opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed"
          }`}
          title={!isAIEnabled ? "Toggle Enhanced AI Writer above to enable" : "AI Write Script"}
        >
          {isGenerating ? (
            <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin" />
          ) : (
            <Sparkles className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          )}
          <span>{isGenerating ? 'Writing...' : 'AI Write Script'}</span>
        </button>

        <button
          onClick={handleAIExtractFrames}
          disabled={!isAIEnabled || isExtracting || !scriptText.trim()}
          className={`flex items-center justify-center gap-1 py-2 rounded-lg text-[10px] font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider transition-all cursor-pointer border ${
            isAIEnabled 
              ? "bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-200 border-neutral-700" 
              : "bg-neutral-900 text-neutral-500 border border-neutral-850/60 opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed"
          }`}
          title={!isAIEnabled ? "Toggle Enhanced AI Writer above to enable" : "Use AI to parse script and extract sequential storyboard shots"}
        >
          {isExtracting ? (
            <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin" />
          ) : (
            <Layers className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-indigo-400" />
          )}
          <span>{isExtracting ? 'Extracting...' : 'AI Extract Shots'}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


========================================
FILE: src/components/UploadModal.tsx
========================================
import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
import {
  Upload, X, Trash2, CheckSquare, Square,
  Image, FileImage, Loader2, FolderTree, ArrowDownToLine
} from 'lucide-react';
import { resizeImage } from '../utils/image';

export interface UploadedFile {
  id: string;
  file: File;
  name: string;
  size: number;
  type: string;
  relativePath: string;
  folder: string;
  dataUrl: string;
  width: number;
  height: number;
  selected: boolean;
  status: 'loading' | 'ready' | 'error';
}

interface UploadModalProps {
  onClose: () => void;
  onImport: (files: UploadedFile[], folderName?: string) => void;
  autoTriggerFolder?: boolean;
}

const ACCEPTED_TYPES = ['image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/gif', 'image/webp', 'image/svg+xml', 'image/bmp'];
const MAX_FILE_SIZE = 50 * 1024 * 1024;

function generateId() {
  return Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10);
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes < 1024) return bytes + ' B';
  if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return (bytes / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB';
  return (bytes / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(1) + ' MB';
}

function extractFolder(path: string): string {
  const parts = path.split('/');
  if (parts.length <= 1) return '';
  return parts.slice(0, -1).join('/');
}

export default function UploadModal({ onClose, onImport, autoTriggerFolder = false }: UploadModalProps) {
  const [uploadedFiles, setUploadedFiles] = useState<UploadedFile[]>([]);
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [detectedFolderName, setDetectedFolderName] = useState('');
  const [isProcessing, setIsProcessing] = useState(false);
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'grid' | 'list'>('grid');
  const [sortBy] = useState<'name' | 'size' | 'folder'>('name');
  const [sortAsc] = useState(true);
  const [filterFolder] = useState<string>('all');

  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const folderInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const dropZoneRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const processFile = useCallback((file: File, relativePath: string): Promise<UploadedFile> => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const id = generateId();
      const folder = extractFolder(relativePath);

      if (!ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) {
        resolve({
          id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
          relativePath, folder, dataUrl: '', width: 0, height: 0,
          selected: false, status: 'error',
        });
        return;
      }

      if (file.size > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
        resolve({
          id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
          relativePath, folder, dataUrl: '', width: 0, height: 0,
          selected: false, status: 'error',
        });
        return;
      }

      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = (e) => {
        const rawDataUrl = e.target?.result as string;
        // Resize image to keep Firestore payload lightweight & robust
        resizeImage(rawDataUrl, 800, 450, 0.55).then((dataUrl) => {
          const img = new window.Image();
          img.onload = () => {
            resolve({
              id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
              relativePath, folder, dataUrl,
              width: img.naturalWidth, height: img.naturalHeight,
              selected: true, status: 'ready',
            });
          };
          img.onerror = () => {
            resolve({
              id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
              relativePath, folder, dataUrl,
              width: 0, height: 0,
              selected: true, status: 'ready',
            });
          };
          img.src = dataUrl;
        }).catch(() => {
          resolve({
            id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
            relativePath, folder, dataUrl: rawDataUrl, width: 0, height: 0,
            selected: true, status: 'ready',
          });
        });
      };
      reader.onerror = () => {
        resolve({
          id, file, name: file.name, size: file.size, type: file.type,
          relativePath, folder, dataUrl: '', width: 0, height: 0,
          selected: false, status: 'error',
        });
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
  }, []);

  const processFiles = useCallback(async (fileList: File[], paths?: string[]) => {
    setIsProcessing(true);
    const results: UploadedFile[] = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < fileList.length; i++) {
      const file = fileList[i];
      const relativePath = paths ? paths[i] : file.name;
      if (!ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) continue;
      const processed = await processFile(file, relativePath);
      results.push(processed);
    }

    setUploadedFiles(prev => [...prev, ...results]);
    setIsProcessing(false);
  }, [processFile]);

  const handleFileSelect = useCallback((e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const files = e.target.files;
    if (!files || files.length === 0) return;
    const fileArray = Array.from(files) as File[];
    const paths = fileArray.map(f => f.name);
    processFiles(fileArray, paths);
    e.target.value = '';
  }, [processFiles]);

  const handleFolderSelect = useCallback(async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const files = e.target.files;
    if (!files || files.length === 0) return;

    const fileArray = Array.from(files) as File[];
    const paths = fileArray.map(f => (f as File & { webkitRelativePath?: string }).webkitRelativePath || f.name);

    let folderName = '';
    for (const p of paths) {
      const parts = p.split('/');
      if (parts.length > 1) { folderName = parts[0]; break; }
    }
    if (folderName) setDetectedFolderName(folderName);

    const results: UploadedFile[] = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < fileArray.length; i++) {
      const file = fileArray[i];
      if (!ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) continue;
      const processed = await processFile(file, paths[i]);
      results.push(processed);
    }

    if (results.length > 0) {
      const readyFiles = results.filter(f => f.status === 'ready');
      if (readyFiles.length > 0) {
        onImport(readyFiles, folderName || undefined);
        onClose();
      }
    }
    e.target.value = '';
  }, [processFile, onImport, onClose]);

  const handleDragEnter = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(true);
  }, []);

  const handleDragLeave = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
    const rect = dropZoneRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (rect) {
      const { clientX, clientY } = e;
      if (clientX < rect.left || clientX > rect.right || clientY < rect.top || clientY > rect.bottom) {
        setIsDragging(false);
      }
    }
  }, []);

  const handleDragOver = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
  }, []);

  const readDirectory = useCallback(async (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry): Promise<{file: File; path: string}[]> => {
    const results: {file: File; path: string}[] = [];

    const readEntries = (dirReader: FileSystemDirectoryReader): Promise<FileSystemEntry[]> => {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => dirReader.readEntries(resolve, reject));
    };

    const getFile = (fileEntry: FileSystemFileEntry): Promise<File> => {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => fileEntry.file(resolve, reject));
    };

    const processEntry = async (e: FileSystemEntry, path: string): Promise<void> => {
      if (e.isFile) {
        try {
          const file = await getFile(e as FileSystemFileEntry);
          if (ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) results.push({ file, path: path + e.name });
        } catch { /* skip */ }
      } else if (e.isDirectory) {
        const dirReader = (e as FileSystemDirectoryEntry).createReader();
        let entries: FileSystemEntry[] = [];
        let batch: FileSystemEntry[];
        do {
          batch = await readEntries(dirReader);
          entries = entries.concat(batch);
        } while (batch.length > 0);

        for (const child of entries) await processEntry(child, path + e.name + '/');
      }
    };

    await processEntry(entry, '');
    return results;
  }, []);

  const handleDrop = useCallback(async (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
    setIsDragging(false); setIsProcessing(true);

    const items = e.dataTransfer.items;
    const allFiles: File[] = [];
    const allPaths: string[] = [];

    if (items) {
      const entries: FileSystemEntry[] = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        const entry = items[i].webkitGetAsEntry?.();
        if (entry) entries.push(entry);
      }

      for (const entry of entries) {
        if (entry.isDirectory) {
          const dirFiles = await readDirectory(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
          for (const { file, path } of dirFiles) { allFiles.push(file); allPaths.push(path); }
        } else if (entry.isFile) {
          const file = await new Promise<File>((resolve, reject) =>
            (entry as FileSystemFileEntry).file(resolve, reject)
          );
          if (ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(file.type)) { allFiles.push(file); allPaths.push(file.name); }
        }
      }
    } else {
      const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
      for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
        if (ACCEPTED_TYPES.includes(files[i].type)) { allFiles.push(files[i]); allPaths.push(files[i].name); }
      }
    }

    if (allFiles.length > 0) await processFiles(allFiles, allPaths);
    setIsProcessing(false);
  }, [processFiles, readDirectory]);

  const toggleSelect = useCallback((id: string) => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.id === id ? { ...f, selected: !f.selected } : f));
  }, []);

  const selectAll = useCallback(() => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.map(f => f.status === 'ready' ? { ...f, selected: true } : f));
  }, []);

  const deselectAll = useCallback(() => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.map(f => ({ ...f, selected: false })));
  }, []);

  const removeFile = useCallback((id: string) => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => f.id !== id));
  }, []);

  const removeAll = useCallback(() => setUploadedFiles([]), []);

  const removeSelected = useCallback(() => {
    setUploadedFiles(prev => prev.filter(f => !f.selected));
  }, []);

  const filteredFiles = uploadedFiles
    .filter(f => filterFolder === 'all' || f.folder === filterFolder || (filterFolder === '' && !f.folder))
    .sort((a, b) => {
      let cmp = 0;
      if (sortBy === 'name') cmp = a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
      else if (sortBy === 'size') cmp = a.size - b.size;
      else if (sortBy === 'folder') cmp = a.folder.localeCompare(b.folder);
      return sortAsc ? cmp : -cmp;
    });

  const selectedCount = uploadedFiles.filter(f => f.selected && f.status === 'ready').length;
  const readyCount = uploadedFiles.filter(f => f.status === 'ready').length;
  const totalSize = uploadedFiles.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0);

  const handleImport = () => {
    const selected = uploadedFiles.filter(f => f.selected && f.status === 'ready');
    if (selected.length > 0) {
      onImport(selected, detectedFolderName || undefined);
      onClose();
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (autoTriggerFolder && folderInputRef.current) {
      folderInputRef.current.click();
    }
  }, [autoTriggerFolder]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = (e: KeyboardEvent) => { if (e.key === 'Escape') onClose(); };
    window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
  }, [onClose]);

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-[#0A0A0B]/90 z-[150] flex items-center justify-center p-4 animate-fade-in backdrop-blur-sm">
      <div className="bg-[#0C0C0E] border border-neutral-800 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-5xl max-h-[90vh] flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-4 border-b border-neutral-800 shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 bg-indigo-600/20 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center"><Upload className="w-4.5 h-4.5 text-indigo-400" /></div>
            <div>
              <h2 className="text-sm font-extrabold text-white tracking-tight">Import Media Files</h2>
              <p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 font-medium">Upload images or drag folders</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="p-2 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-400 hover:text-neutral-200 rounded-lg transition-colors"><X className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
        </div>

        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden flex flex-col">
          <div className="px-5 py-4 border-b border-neutral-800/60 shrink-0">
            <div ref={dropZoneRef} onDragEnter={handleDragEnter} onDragLeave={handleDragLeave} onDragOver={handleDragOver} onDrop={handleDrop} onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}
              className={`relative border-2 border-dashed rounded-xl p-6 text-center transition-all cursor-pointer ${isDragging ? 'border-indigo-500 bg-indigo-500/10 scale-[1.01]' : 'border-neutral-700 bg-neutral-800/30 hover:border-neutral-600 hover:bg-neutral-800/50'}`}>
              {isProcessing ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2"><Loader2 className="w-8 h-8 text-indigo-400 animate-spin" /><p className="text-xs text-indigo-300 font-bold">Processing...</p></div>
              ) : isDragging ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2"><ArrowDownToLine className="w-8 h-8 text-indigo-400 animate-bounce" /><p className="text-xs text-indigo-300 font-bold">Drop here</p></div>
              ) : (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-neutral-800 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center border border-neutral-700"><FileImage className="w-5 h-5 text-neutral-400" /></div>
                    <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-neutral-800 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center border border-neutral-700"><FolderTree className="w-5 h-5 text-neutral-400" /></div>
                  </div>
                  <div><p className="text-xs text-neutral-300 font-bold">Drag & drop images or folders</p><p className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 mt-0.5">Supports PNG, JPG, GIF, WebP, SVG, BMP</p></div>
                </div>
              )}
              <input ref={fileInputRef} type="file" multiple accept="image/*" onChange={handleFileSelect} className="hidden" />
              <input ref={folderInputRef} type="file" {...({webkitdirectory: "true", directory: "true"} as React.InputHTMLAttributes<HTMLInputElement>)} multiple onChange={handleFolderSelect} className="hidden" />
            </div>

            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-3">
              <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); fileInputRef.current?.click(); }} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold transition-colors border border-neutral-700"><Image className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Files</button>
              <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); folderInputRef.current?.click(); }} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold transition-colors border border-neutral-700"><FolderTree className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Folder</button>

              {uploadedFiles.length > 0 && (
                <>
                  <div className="h-4 w-px bg-neutral-700 mx-1" />
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 font-mono">{uploadedFiles.length} files • {formatFileSize(totalSize)}</span>
                </>
              )}

              {uploadedFiles.length > 0 && (
                <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="flex bg-neutral-800 rounded-lg border border-neutral-700 overflow-hidden">
                    <button onClick={() => setViewMode('grid')} className={`px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-bold ${viewMode === 'grid' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400'}`}>Grid</button>
                    <button onClick={() => setViewMode('list')} className={`px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-bold ${viewMode === 'list' ? 'bg-indigo-600 text-white' : 'text-neutral-400'}`}>List</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-5 py-3">
            {uploadedFiles.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="flex-1">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3 sticky top-0 bg-[#0C0C0E] py-1.5 z-10">
                  <button onClick={selectedCount === readyCount ? deselectAll : selectAll} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 bg-neutral-800 hover:bg-neutral-700 text-neutral-300 rounded text-[10px] font-bold border border-neutral-700">
                    {selectedCount === readyCount ? <CheckSquare className="w-3 h-3 text-indigo-400" /> : <Square className="w-3 h-3" />} {selectedCount === readyCount ? 'Deselect All' : 'Select All'}
                  </button>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <button onClick={removeSelected} disabled={selectedCount === 0} className="text-[10px] text-rose-400 font-bold disabled:opacity-30">Remove Selected</button>
                    <button onClick={removeAll} className="text-[10px] text-neutral-500 font-bold">Clear All</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <FileGrid files={filteredFiles} viewMode={viewMode} onToggle={toggleSelect} onRemove={removeFile} />
              </div>
            ) : !isProcessing && (
              <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center py-12 text-center"><div><Upload className="w-10 h-10 text-neutral-700 mx-auto mb-3" /><p className="text-xs text-neutral-600">No files yet</p></div></div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3 border-t border-neutral-800 bg-neutral-900/80 shrink-0">
          <span className="text-[10px] text-emerald-400 font-bold">{readyCount} ready</span>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button onClick={onClose} className="px-4 py-2 bg-neutral-800 text-neutral-400 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold">Cancel</button>
            <button onClick={handleImport} disabled={selectedCount === 0} className="px-5 py-2 bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded-lg text-xs font-extrabold disabled:opacity-40">Import {selectedCount} Frames</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

interface FileGridProps { files: UploadedFile[]; viewMode: 'grid' | 'list'; onToggle: (id: string) => void; onRemove: (id: string) => void; }

function FileGrid({ files, viewMode, onToggle, onRemove }: FileGridProps) {
  if (viewMode === 'grid') {
    return (
      <div className="grid grid-cols-4 sm:grid-cols-5 md:grid-cols-6 lg:grid-cols-7 gap-2">
        {files.map(f => (
          <div key={f.id} onClick={() => f.status === 'ready' && onToggle(f.id)}
            className={`group relative rounded-lg border overflow-hidden cursor-pointer ${f.status === 'error' ? 'opacity-60 grayscale' : f.selected ? 'border-indigo-500 ring-1 ring-indigo-500/30' : 'border-neutral-700 bg-neutral-800/40'}`}>
            <div className="aspect-square bg-black flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
              {f.dataUrl ? <img src={f.dataUrl} alt={f.name} className="w-full h-full object-cover" /> : <FileImage className="w-6 h-6 text-neutral-700" />}
            </div>
            {f.selected && <div className="absolute top-1 left-1"><CheckSquare className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" /></div>}
            <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onRemove(f.id); }} className="absolute top-1 right-1 p-0.5 bg-black/70 rounded text-neutral-500 hover:text-rose-400 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"><X className="w-3 h-3" /></button>
            <div className="px-1.5 py-1 bg-neutral-900/90"><p className="text-[9px] text-neutral-300 truncate font-medium">{f.name}</p></div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    );
  }
  return (
    <div className="space-y-1">
      {files.map(f => (
        <div key={f.id} onClick={() => f.status === 'ready' && onToggle(f.id)}
          className={`flex items-center gap-3 p-2 rounded-lg cursor-pointer ${f.selected ? 'bg-indigo-500/10 border border-indigo-500/30' : 'bg-neutral-800/30 border border-transparent'}`}>
          {f.selected ? <CheckSquare className="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-400" /> : <Square className="w-4 h-4 text-neutral-600" />}
          <div className="w-10 h-8 rounded bg-black border border-neutral-700 overflow-hidden shrink-0 flex items-center justify-center">
            {f.dataUrl ? <img src={f.dataUrl} alt={f.name} className="w-full h-full object-cover" /> : <FileImage className="w-4 h-4 text-neutral-700" />}
          </div>
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0"><p className="text-[11px] text-neutral-200 truncate font-medium">{f.name}</p></div>
          <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onRemove(f.id); }} className="p-1 text-neutral-600 hover:text-rose-400"><Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /></button>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

import { clsx, type ClassValue } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}


========================================
FILE: src/utils/image.ts
========================================
export function resizeImage(dataUrl: string, maxWidth: number = 1024, maxHeight: number = 720, quality: number = 0.75): Promise<string> {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const img = new Image();
    img.onload = () => {
      let width = img.width;
      let height = img.height;

      if (width > maxWidth || height > maxHeight) {
        const ratio = Math.min(maxWidth / width, maxHeight / height);
        width = Math.round(width * ratio);
        height = Math.round(height * ratio);
      }

      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      canvas.width = width;
      canvas.height = height;

      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (ctx) {
        ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, width, height);
        // Convert to JPEG for maximum compression
        resolve(canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', quality));
      } else {
        resolve(dataUrl);
      }
    };
    img.onerror = () => {
      resolve(dataUrl);
    };
    img.src = dataUrl;
  });
}
